Sudden Death While Drinking Tea in a Teahouse 137

Li Pansheng, a 41-year-old native of Suzhou, was formerly a team leader number 136 in the French Concession police force. He lived at number 6 of the Baixiang Village on Father Rhodes Road. After resigning from his police duties, he went to the Huxinting Teahouse in the City God Temple every day. He would walk around the temple for a week and then go up to the pavilion to drink tea at about 4 o'clock. About half an hour later, Li suddenly collapsed on the table. The tea room attendant thought he was just tired and dozing off. It wasn't until about 5:30 that the attendant saw that Li had not woken up. The attendant called out to him but received no response, and realizing that something was wrong, he quickly went downstairs to report to the police, who relayed the report to the City God Temple police station and had Li taken to the hospital for treatment. However, he had already died before he could be taken downstairs. Someone rushed to Li's house to report to his wife, Mrs. Du (30 years old, from Pudong), who led her son and daughter to the scene, weeping over the body. Mrs. Du claimed that Li only had stomach problems in the past, and his sudden death was completely unexpected.

Conference of the Beijing-Shanghai, Tianjin-Pukou, and Beijing-Ning Railways on Improving Through Train Service between Shanghai and Beijing 139

Thirty Proposals in Five Categories

Decision to Continue Discussions Today

The Beijing-Shanghai, Tianjin-Pukou, and Beijing-Ning Railways, following the Ministry's order to improve through train service between Shanghai and Beijing, held a conference at the Shanghai North Station's Traffic Office starting at 10:00 AM yesterday. Details are recorded below:

Order from the Ministry of Railways

The Beijing-Shanghai, Tianjin-Pukou, and Beijing-Ning Railways: Following the Ministry of Railways' instructions, it is noted that the Shanghai-Beijing through train service operates between the commercial hub of Shanghai and the cultural center of Beijing. The route is extensive, spanning north and south. It is frequented by foreign diplomats, industrial survey groups, and international tourists. All facilities are therefore closely related to international perception, and their importance is well-known. The Ministry has repeatedly ordered thorough improvements on record. It is now found that the service is generally orderly and well-equipped. However, aspects such as the cleanliness of equipment, punctuality of schedules, the service spirit of on-board staff, and management methods should be vigorously improved to enhance passenger comfort and gradually match the most perfect passenger trains in the world, thereby enhancing international reputation and increasing the glory of the railways. In addition to separate orders, you are hereby urgently instructed to promptly confer on detailed improvement measures, to be submitted for review and decision, without negligence. This order.

Three-Way Conference

The three-way conference was held at the Shanghai North Station starting at 10:00 AM yesterday. Attendees included Xiao Weiguo, Chief of the Traffic Office of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway; Wang Zhigang, Deputy Chief; Wang Shuchun, Chief of the Su-Song Section Traffic Division; Li Jingwei, Director of the Dispatching Section of the Transportation Department; Shen Zunli, Director of the Passenger Transportation Section of the Business Department; Wu Yukun, Senior Engineer of the Beijing-Dan Section of the Mechanical Department; Li Xizhi, Senior Engineer of the Su-Song Section; Zhong Yanglin, Assistant Mechanical Engineer; Chen Shungeng, Chief of the Traffic Office of the Tianjin-Pukou Railway; Wang Jiqiu, Director of the Dispatching Section of the Transportation Department; Li Quansun, Director of the Passenger Transportation Section of the Business Department; Pan Shining, Assistant Mechanical Engineer of the Mechanical Department; Tan Changyuehuan, Deputy Director of the Transportation Department of the Beijing-Ning Railway Traffic Office; Wang Zhengcang, Chief of the Passenger Section of the Business Department; and Hua Hannian, Chief of the Tianjin Locomotive Section of the Mechanical Department. Chief Xiao chaired the meeting, and Tang Xiongjie served as the recorder.

Categorized Discussion

A total of thirty proposals were discussed in five categories. The proposals are recorded as follows: 1. Exchange blueprints of the structure and equipment of carriages on each railway for through train service. 2. Re-number the berth numbers. 3. Improve the toilets in the second and third-class carriages. 4. Install tea rooms in all third-class carriages. 5. Install screens and electric fans in third-class carriages during the summer to enhance passenger comfort. 6. Improve the connection structure at both ends of third-class carriages to enhance safety. 7. Operate third-class sleeping cars on the Shanghai-Beijing through train. 8. Improve baggage and mail cars and standardize internal structural designs. 9. Install air brake switches on all brake vans to ensure safe train operation. 10. Install side lights on all baggage and mail brake vans. 11. Standardize the seating arrangement for on-board military police. 12. Pay attention to the cleanliness of curtains, bedding, and mirror frames inside the carriages. 13. The Beijing-Ning and Beijing-Shanghai Railways should be responsible for minor repairs of Tianjin-Pukou carriages during operation. 14. If carriages from any railway are damaged within another railway's section and impede operation, the local railway should immediately replace them. 15. Construct covered sheds specifically for storing Shanghai-Beijing through trains after arrival. 16. The uniforms for first, second, and third-class car attendants should be consistent across all railways. 17. After the Beijing-Shanghai train of the Shanghai-Beijing through train arrives at Nanjing Station, reduce one third-class carriage to standardize and save engine power. 18. Decide at which station the undercarriage should be parked overnight. 19. Establish standard procedures for adding private or special cars to the Shanghai-Beijing through train and determine the maximum number of carriages allowed. 20. How should the composition and order of connection of carriages on each through train be determined to facilitate work and convenience passengers? 21. How should passengers' baggage be restricted to maintain order? 22. How should the order of seating for first and second-class passengers be maintained? 23. Passengers boarding to see off or greet others often enter carriages to search, disrupting order. How should this be restricted to maintain order? 24. How should the segmented charging method for tea inside each train be thoroughly implemented to prevent corruption? 26. The training methods for attendants inside each train should be agreed upon by the three railways and implemented jointly on the same principle to facilitate implementation. 27. On-board supervisors should adjust the temperature inside the carriages at any time to ensure comfort. 28. Improve dining car service. 29. Issue parcel tickets for the Shanghai-Beijing through train to benefit passengers. 30. Improve the reservation method for sleeping berths.

After the Haichang Company's Sea Peace vessel collided with the British Asia Oil vessel in Yingkou and sank, it has now been proven that the Sea Peace accident was caused by the ship turning its hull, resulting in the collision with the British vessel. Approximately Thirty Years Old

Russian Vendetta Case 143

The Deceased Was Once a Chinese Soldier

Killed for Embezzling Military Pay

Russian national Lavr Lavrov Nikola (transliteration), 34 years old, had recently arrived in Shanghai from Tianjin, only about ten days ago. On the evening of the 3rd of this month, around 10 PM, he was suddenly attacked in Lane 855 of Avenue Joffre in the French Concession by a fellow Russian, Piyan Jinxia Guv (transliteration, 29 years old), who pulled out a sharp blade and stabbed him three times in the back before fleeing. After being injured, Lavr sought treatment at the Public Hospital on North Suzhou Road and reported the incident to the French police, who arrested the suspect. Lavr died at the Public Hospital at 0:30 AM on the 13th due to internal injuries. The hospital notified the French police, who transported the body to the Autopsy Department affiliated with the Municipal Council Hospital on Talus Road. Yesterday, the Second Special Court dispatched Prosecutor Wang Ren, along with a forensic doctor, clerk, interpreter, etc., to the hospital at noon to confirm that the deceased had died from knife wounds sustained during his lifetime. As the deceased had no relatives in Shanghai, the court ordered that the body be buried by the Municipal Council Charity Association. The police then transferred the suspect, Piyan Jinxia Guv, to the First Criminal Tribunal of the Second Special Court. Judge Cao Jun presided over the hearing. According to the police lawyer, Yao Zhao, the defendant was charged with murder. The police requested an extension as the investigation was not yet complete, and the defendant would be detained pending further investigation. The defendant confessed that he and the deceased had both served in the Chinese army in Shandong. The deceased was the captain, and he was a soldier. He claimed that the deceased embezzled military pay and beat him. After the army disbanded, the deceased fled to Tianjin and other places, and he followed him, determined to seek revenge. The court verified the confession and postponed the trial to the 23rd for further investigation. The defendant was returned to custody.

Five Baskets of Copper Coins 144

With Hidden Compartments

More Than Two Hundred Coins in Total

Wenzhou natives Wei Yongchang, Wen Baoshan, and Su Yida, used copper coins at the Tianyun Building in the Wing On Company on the evening of the 30th of last month when dealing with small vendors. A total of two hundred and twenty-nine copper coins were discovered in the compartments. They were transferred to the First Special Court. According to the confessions, the copper coins were purchased from a Sun Baojin for thirty yuan for every hundred yuan in copper coins, which they brought to Shanghai to use. After arguments between the police lawyer Wang Yaotang and the defendant's lawyer, Judge Qian Hongye ordered them to be detained pending sentencing.

Special Feature: Several Fundamental Issues of the Chinese Constitution (3) 157

— Recorded by Fan Shiqin

Speech by Mr. Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan

The Five-Yuan System and the President: The five-yuan system of the central government is different in the draft constitution from the current system. Currently, the government is organized by the Kuomintang. The chairman of the current National Government is the head of state, but in reality, he has no power. The draft constitution stipulates that the supreme head of state is the president, who has the highest actual power. Some people believe that the president's power is too high and borders on dictatorship, but the president is elected by the people, and the people have the power to impeach him. At the same time, the Legislative Yuan exercises legislative power, which will not allow the president to become a dictator. If the legislative power is also in the hands of the president, then the president will become the sole holder of both legislative and executive power, which would be dictatorship. Or, if the parliament is the president's parliament, like in Germany, it would also become a dictatorship. In a country ruled by law, if the administrative head has new policies, it needs to promulgate laws. If the budget changes, it must first be approved by the Legislative Yuan before it can be implemented. Otherwise, it cannot be changed. All other laws are the same and cannot be changed. The head of state has a high position in the country, but still needs the consent of the Legislative Yuan to make decisions. The Legislative Yuan is a state organ, and the president is the sole leader of the state, but his policies must be supported by the people and approved by the Legislative Yuan. It cannot be said to be dictatorial politics.

In the future, when the constitution is established and the five-yuan constitution is implemented, the future president will definitely be the leader of the majority party and will naturally be supported by the people. If a party occupies a majority among the people, then the president elected by that party will be approved by the people. The president's policies are subject to the approval of the Legislative Yuan, and the Legislative Yuan will not deliberately make things difficult for the president. The president can then lead the five yuan to work, but the five yuan are not subject to the president's control. For example, we know that Germany and Italy have both formed governments through bloodless revolutions. Mussolini of Italy is the leader of the Fascist Party. Although Mussolini has great power, he is not the emperor. All power does not reside in Mussolini's leadership. The Italian government is organized by the Fascist Party, but when Mussolini decides a policy, it must also be passed by the parliament. It cannot be considered a dictatorship in essence (to be continued).

Zhongshan Native Association

Express mail telegram to Your Excellency Minister of Transportation: We have received a statement from Ms. Li Bingyan, a member of our association and a graduate of our college, stating that on the 4th of this month, she traveled from Guangzhou to Shanghai on the China Merchants Bureau's Wuyi steamer. When the ship docked in Shantou, the ship's captain, a Norwegian named Norguistott, forcibly pried open her door and attempted an indecent assault. He was spotted and stopped. Unexpectedly, on the second night, he still secretly went to the original room to plot wrongdoing. Fortunately, she had reported this to the acting second mate of the ship, Zhang Huoyan, who switched rooms, thus avoiding the disaster. Considering that the China Merchants Bureau is a state-owned shipping bureau under your jurisdiction, it is unacceptable to allow foreign crew members to commit such indecent acts, which undermines the safety of travelers and damages national dignity. We hereby telegram Your Excellency Minister, requesting you to promptly order the China Merchants Bureau to investigate, dismiss, and severely punish the perpetrator to deter evildoers. This is our earnest plea. Shanghai National Medical Association Chinese Medical College, respectfully. 2. Letter to the China Merchants Bureau: We are writing to you that we have received a statement from Ms. Li Bingyan, a member of our association and a graduate of our college, stating that on the 4th of this month, she traveled from Guangzhou to Shanghai on the China Merchants Bureau's Wuyi steamer. When the ship docked in Shantou, the ship's captain, a Norwegian named Norguistott, forcibly pried open her door and attempted an indecent assault. He was spotted and stopped. Unexpectedly, on the second night, he still secretly went to the original room to plot wrongdoing. Fortunately, she had reported this to the acting second mate of the ship, Zhang Huoyan, who switched rooms, thus avoiding the disaster. This is outrageous. Your bureau is a state-owned enterprise, and you should ensure the safety of travelers and maintain your reputation. Ms. Li's report has been verified by acting second mate Zhang. If it is true, and you do not severely dismiss and punish the perpetrator, how will your bureau face the passengers and how will you protect national dignity? We hereby send this letter to request that your bureau promptly investigate and severely punish the perpetrator to safeguard your shipping reputation. This is in the public interest. Respectfully addressed to General Manager Liu of the China Merchants Bureau. Shanghai National Medical Association Chinese Medical College.

Liu Hongsheng States According to the New News Agency's reporter, the General Manager of the China Merchants Bureau, Liu Hongsheng, stated that the Wuyi steamer is not owned by the bureau, and its original agent was the Yuan'an Shipping Company. The bureau leased the steamer from Yuan'an Company, and the ship's captain was also appointed by Yuan'an. All navigation certificates were issued by the Maritime Affairs Bureau. It is unfortunate that the ship's captain, a Norwegian named Norguistott, attempted to rape a passenger. However, Ms. Li Bingyan has not yet reported to the bureau, and the details are not yet known. The bureau cannot consider any measures to be taken. Although the ship's captain was not appointed by the bureau, if Ms. Li reports to the bureau and the investigation confirms the incident, the bureau has the right to request the original ship owner, Yuan'an Company, to replace the captain.

Attitude of the Maritime Affairs Bureau The New News Agency reporter subsequently visited Mr. Chen Xianyan, Secretary of the Maritime Affairs Bureau, and inquired about the bureau's disciplinary measures for the Norwegian captain of the Wuyi steamer, Norguistott, who attempted to rape a passenger. According to him, after the case was reported in the newspapers, the bureau paid close attention to it. However, the person involved, Ms. Li Bingyan, has not yet reported to the bureau, and the China Merchants Bureau has not submitted a report either. Therefore, the bureau has not been able to investigate the matter. Once Ms. Li Bingyan reports to the bureau, the bureau will thoroughly investigate the facts at the time and take appropriate action.

Shen Bao National Products Weekly

Words of Contribution

Announcement to Readers 159

— The Editor

Our publication has been meeting with readers for nearly two years and has received much support, for which we are extremely grateful. However, we believe that promoting national products cannot be achieved through empty words alone, nor can it be promoted through ideals alone. The colleagues deeply feel that the articles in our publication have been too focused on empty theories and lacked practical content, too lengthy and lacking in concise and insightful points, and the words and actions have not been in accordance, and the intentions have not been relevant, which has made it difficult to satisfy the readers' wishes. In the future, the style will be slightly changed, focusing on short articles that investigate the actual situation and incisive and accurate criticisms, without relying on empty words and with supporting evidence. Each article should be lively and interesting with four to five hundred words. Lengthy articles and empty, superficial words will be omitted, and two columns will be added to increase interest.

1. National Products Investigation Records: The production and sales of national products in various regions, the progress of national product industries, and the people's views on national products will be described separately, with concise language. These short articles are very welcome.

2. Introduction of New Products from Various Factories: If there are any new products from various factories, or if there are any special points that can be used by consumers to compete with foreign products, please inform us. After our publication investigates and confirms them and reviews them as qualified, we are willing to disclose them to the people of the country.

In addition, photos and illustrations are also welcome.

Patriot Pan Zhishi and National Products 160

— The Editor

Patriot Pan Hongsheng was arrested for opposing unscrupulous merchants selling imported goods, subjected to electric torture, and eventually died. On the day of Pan Zhishi's funeral, we witnessed the grand procession of various sectors escorting the funeral, stretching for miles. We believe that Pan Zhishi's willingness to die, disregarding his life, to fight unscrupulous merchants is unattainable, but his spirit is immortal. The whole city offered incense, and his honor is also unattainable. Preserving the righteous spirit of the world and reclaiming national personality, Pan Zhishi's death is of great value and adds countless protections to the future of national products. The curses against unscrupulous merchants in the funeral procession, wishing to get their due, were heard everywhere. In the future, unscrupulous merchants who sell imported goods will be intimidated, their conscience will be restored, or they will slightly reduce their activities of selling imported goods by changing their appearances. Recently, intimidated by the vigilance of the anti-traitor group and frightened by the mourning of the kneeling and crying group, they should put down the butcher knife and embark on the right path. What in the world is impossible to do? What money cannot be earned? It is unreasonable to deliberately abandon conscience and risk impropriety to sell imported goods for profit. It is our sincere hope that those who have committed this will have a moment of conscience and awaken, so that Pan Zhishi's death will not be in vain.

National Products Proposal

Suggesting the First Step of Industry Association 161

— He Gongxing

It is well known that industry association is a good remedy to rescue the current national products industry. However, this problem is not easy to solve. There are many conflicts of interest and personnel involvement. Different concepts and different purposes, and other kinds of facilities, are all obstacles to association. Is it because the time has not come? Then the national products industry has long been reduced to fratricide and will become a bankrupt situation. Is it because the people in it have not yet awakened? Then you can often see people running around and telling each other that they are sad that the industry is not cooperating and there is no way to do it, and sigh that it is an incurable disease. In general, everyone hopes that the industry will unite, but everyone dares not unite with the industry. To be fair, it is difficult to start a business, so it is difficult to lightly try the old one. Moreover, the four words "peer jealousy" have not only become a fixed name in the business community for hundreds of years, but also become a settled situation. The image is too bad and it is not easy to eliminate. Therefore, the problem of industry association has always become a pending case, and there is only empty talk and no way to implement it. If we prescribe the right medicine, we should first explain the points of suspicion of both parties, lead the interests according to the situation, and come gradually. Then there is the first step of the industry association suggestion.

1. Joint procurement: When factories purchase raw materials or consumables, it is of course cheaper to buy in bulk than to buy in retail. The same industries need the same goods. This can be combined. Even if the quantity is different, it can be apportioned according to the proportion. In the past, the same goods were different from factory A and factory B. The products this year were different from last year, and the first product was different from the second product. Why? They are all put together from all sides when purchasing raw materials, and there is no standardization. In this way, not only are raw materials cheap, or the cost is low, but if a large batch of orders are sent out, they will not be returned because they are different from the sample. By this, the competition between industries can also be avoided, and it is even more important for the future of national product sales.

2. Joint storage: The factory storage is originally used to store raw and cooked goods, just like the vault of the silver industry. The relationship is very important. The factory addresses of the same industries are not necessarily close to each other, and there is no need to be close to each other. The storage address must be chosen in a quiet place, with convenient water and land transportation, thorough fire protection, suitable houses, and stable management. If each factory has its own storage, the houses may not be suitable, and it is also too uneconomical. Fortunately, raw and cooked goods belong to the same category. Since there is no reason not to disclose secrets, why not gather them in one place? You can get many benefits. In case of financial difficulties, you can also get many conveniences by mortgaging to the bank. In other cases, insurance can be jointly insured, staff can be shared, and trucks and boats can be jointly purchased. This can not only promote the business association of the same industries, but also save many economic spirits for each factory.

3. Joint branch offices in other places: The business of branch offices in other places of each factory is mainly based on retail sales, and there is relatively little conflict of interest. If there are no industries in the local area, there is no need for competition. Since there is no competition, how can it not be combined? Since it does not matter the sales volume, it can save many expenses. If there are local industries, they should be combined. At the beginning, the strength is great, and the advantages and disadvantages are self-evident. People from the same hometown are closer in other places. What about the same industries?

4. Joint production: The so-called joint production is to limit production. The scarcity of goods makes them expensive, and the abundance of goods makes them cheap. In recent years, the reason why national product factories in various industries at sea are desperately depreciating prices and competing for sales, regardless of their capital, is all caused by the excess of products. The cause of the disease is where it should be treated. Please be safe and do not be impatient. Within the possible scope, limit production individually. If you can get the help of the local government and come out to control it, it is even more fair. Our national products cannot be sold to foreign countries as a dumping ground. Even if they are sold with small profits but large sales, they belong to the national economy. It only shows that they are greedy and have no pressure. Do they want to control an industry?

5. Joint customers: In recent years, the market situation has been deteriorating, and customers have continued to go bankrupt. Often, a small customer is bankrupted to tens of thousands of gold. In one industry, tens of thousands or eighty thousand gold are bankrupted. The reason is mostly caused by the lack of association in the industry. If a certain customer owes me three thousand gold, it seems that I can trust him. How do I know that in ten other industries in the same industry, he owes three thousand gold each? Everyone thinks that he can trust him. Once he goes bankrupt, he will regret it. If you want to inquire with each other at ordinary times, it is difficult to do it in fact before the industry is united in business. The secret is not enough, and people abandon what I take, which is even more the business method of the era of overproduction. Now, if the receivable account of the customer is due, but it has not been received, or it is deliberately delayed, or the check that has been paid is returned when it is due, then the customer is no longer a good customer, and the name of the customer and the amount owed should be notified to the industry so that everyone will pay attention.

6. Joint competitions: When exhibitions are held in various places, each factory in the industry should select fine products and participate together. This is enough to show the spirit of an industry and gather ideas. It will definitely win a lot of applause. At ordinary times, you can also choose a date to hold an exhibition of products from the same industry to compare the level of craftsmanship. For example, the cosmetics exhibition held by the Home Industry Society recently, Mr. Yang Yan called it the beginning of industry cooperation, which is a famous saying.

7. Temporary association: In recent years, those who are enthusiastic about national products have spared no effort in promoting the use of national products. National product temporary markets are held in various places without interruption. Whenever you encounter this kind of business to join, you should join together with the industry. Before joining, you should first gather people in the industry or technical experts to evaluate the goods, estimate the prices, trade fairly, and let people choose and buy. After the temporary market is over, the industry can also be held alone. Even if the products are sometimes overproduced, it is not difficult to make them demand greater than supply. In this way, one by one is united, and the industry is almost close to united business.

National Products Discussion

The Fundamental Way to Promote National Products 162

— Zhu Weixuan

Except for a part of specialized people who are obsessed with Europeanization, and whose clothing, food, housing, and transportation are all non-foreign, they are indeed insane and unforgivable. As for the rest of the majority of compatriots who use foreign goods, I believe that although there are also a few who worship foreign goods and are willing to let the profits flow out, it is undeniable that China's industry and commerce are backward and there is no supply of corresponding substitutes!

If you don't believe me, weren't the tooth powders popular in our country a few years ago all Japanese goods such as Diamond and Lion Brand? At that time, especially Diamond tooth powder, almost all rural women and children knew it, from which it can be seen that its history of spreading in our country is long and common! However, in recent years, the Invincible Tooth Powder and Toothpaste of the Home Industry Society, and the Samsung Toothpaste of the China Chemical Society, have excellent quality and have come from behind, so the enemy's tooth powder has been naturally eliminated without boycott.

There are also condiments necessary for home cooking. In the past, only enemy goods [Ajinomoto] sold well in the market. Now, it has been taken over by the MSG of the Tianchu Factory and the Weisheng of the China Chemical Society. The Japanese goods [Ajinomoto] have almost disappeared from the market!

From the above two obvious examples, we can know that the people of our country do not necessarily love to use foreign goods. It is really because there are no corresponding substitutes in our country!

Newspaper propaganda, meetings, speeches, and other national product promotion movements, I think they are all temporary solutions. Only when the Chinese people imitate imported goods and improve national products to replace foreign goods, that is the wonderful way to cure the root cause. At this time, there will be perfect national products, and the people will not need you to publicize and persuade them to use them, and they will be happy to buy them. After all, the Chinese people's vision is narrow, and the national concept is even more very indifferent. Unless there is a supply of actual substitutes, the future of the national product movement will be difficult to get bright!

However, seeking substitutes for national products is not an easy task. We poor boys are incapable of it. This must be done by a general group of industrialists, and at the same time, the government should also provide special protection to national product factories, urging and encouraging them to produce and improve. Tooth powder and MSG are just like a drop in the ocean in our country's products. All other foreign goods need to be replaced by national products. Here, I sincerely hope that the general industrialists will work hard to move forward! [Tooth Powder] [MSG] are a good example for you! Work hard! There will definitely be considerable gains!

An Effective Way to Eliminate Foreign Envelopes and Stationery 163

— Chu Jianping

My classmate Qin is a veteran among post office employees. Yesterday, he told me a story. Although it is inevitable that it is a little mischievous, it is very refreshing to talk about it on the basis of promoting national products.

Qin Jun said: [The Chinese people's superstition of using foreign goods has not diminished to this day. This can be seen in the mail we handle. I dare not lie! Among a package of mail, at least more than a hundred are pure foreign envelopes, red, red, green, and green, like the business cards of a book building; some even want to be fleshy and numb, sprinkled with some Paris perfume, which is really the best of enchantments. Therefore, I pre-engraved a wooden seal with the words: [This is a foreign envelope, users should know to be ashamed], and picked it up on foreign envelopes one by one and stamped it one by one, so that the recipient can notify the sender to change it. I think this is very effective!]

After listening to Qin Jun's words, I admired his enthusiasm and courage very much, so I wrote it out to warn the compatriots all over the country not to humiliate themselves again. At the same time, I have to advise our pen-holding comrades that you must not use foreign envelope paper when writing the text of the National Products Weekly in the future, otherwise, no matter how well your work is written, the editor will not be able to cut it off and throw it into the wastebasket!

Subsidy for Northeastern Students Changes to Recommendation Form 168

Schools in various mountains are responsible for filling out and submitting

The Northeastern Youth Education Relief Office of the Ministry of Education, for Northeastern youth studying in the country, previously had students fill out application forms and have them certified by the schools where they were located. Under this method, the schools would certify all application forms filled out by students in the current year. Now, the Northeastern Youth Education Relief Office has changed the application form to a recommendation form and issued the forms to various schools, based on the actual situation of Northeastern students in the school, to be filled out and registered responsibly, which is more accurate and thorough than having students fill out freely, so as not to have abuse. The recommendation form is being prepared by the office in Beiping and will be sent to all provinces and cities across the country within a few days. Generally, schools above the specialized level will fill out the forms and send them directly to the office, while elementary and middle schools will send them to the office through the education departments and bureaus of each province and city. The office will review them and send personnel to investigate and confirm that they meet the subsidy standards, and then provide subsidy funds accordingly.

Overseas Chinese Elementary and Middle Schools Temporarily Exempt from Joint Examination 169

The Ministry of Education recently replied to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, saying that it agreed that overseas Chinese elementary and middle schools should be temporarily exempted from the joint graduation examination before the regulations for the joint examination of students in overseas Chinese elementary and middle schools are promulgated. The Ministry and the Commission will soon jointly issue orders to the consulates and embassies abroad to notify them separately.

Preparations to Establish 20th Anniversary Celebration

The Chinese Science Society held its first board meeting after the annual meeting at the Biological Research Institute of the Society on Chengxian Street, Nanjing, at 6:00 PM on the 11th of this month. Directors Bing Nongshan, Zhu Kezhen, Hu Gangfu, Zhou Zijing, Yang Yunzhong, Zhao Yuanren, Sun Hongfen, Ren Shuyong, Weng Wenhao, Hu Buzeng, and Wu Liande attended. Bing Nongshan chaired the meeting. Song Hanzhang, a member of the Fund Management Committee, resigned due to old age and physical frailty. It was proposed to publicly elect a successor. The resolution was to ask Mr. Song Hanzhang to reluctantly continue in his role. If the burden proves too great, Mr. Cai Yuanpei would be requested to ask Mr. Qian Xinliu, a member of the Fund Management Committee, to share the responsibilities. 2. Regarding the selection of the head of the Editorial Department of the Society, it was resolved that after the Society's scientific journal had been published for eighteen years, and with the original head of the Editorial Department, Wang Jiliang, going abroad, Dr. Liu Xian, the head of the Biology Department of Shandong University, would be specifically appointed as his successor, and would be stationed at the Society full-time to take charge of the work. 3. Regarding the editing of the Scientific Series, it was resolved to proceed according to the original plan. Regarding how to commemorate the 20th anniversary of the establishment of the Society next year, it was resolved to: 1. hold an achievement exhibition; 2. publish a commemorative album of the Society's overview and a book entitled "Scientific National Rejuvenation"; 3. hold one event in Shanghai in mid-August before the annual meeting, and another in Nanjing on October 25th. 5. Regarding the nomination of the next annual meeting's paper committee, it was resolved to nominate Wang Jiaji, Qian Yunong, Zhang Qiyun, Zeng Zhaolun, Liang Zhengzhi, Zhu Kezhen, Weng Wenhao, Zhang Yun, and Wang Xinggong as members. 6. Regarding how to reorganize local alumni associations, which often lack responsible personnel due to the departure of staff, it was resolved that the Nanjing Alumni Association would be convened by the directors stationed in Beijing, and the Suzhou and Hangzhou locations would be convened by the original secretaries of the alumni associations, and that staff would be elected every two years. 7. Regarding the proposal to invite science students from universities in various regions, who mostly have scientific society organizations, to join as group members of the Society, but the Society's constitution has no provisions for this, it was resolved to amend the constitution, and Yang Yunzhong, Hu Gangfu, and Zhou Zijing were appointed as drafting committee members for the amendment of the constitution. Other proposals were briefly discussed, and the meeting adjourned.

A Visit to the Shanghai Library School, a Militarized School 175

Founded by Li Shizeng and Wu Zhihui

Implementing a New Education of Learning While Working

A Truly New Lived-in School

The Shanghai Library School was jointly founded by Li Shizeng, Wu Zhihui, and others from the Chinese International Library, in cooperation with the World Book Company. The school is located on Longjiang Road, Yangshupu. As the school's system is different from ordinary schools, our reporter specially drove to visit it yesterday. The details of what was learned are recorded as follows:

Founding Process The school is named the Library School, with the aim of cultivating practical cultural talents with balanced development of experience and knowledge through the method of mutual participation and advancement of work and academics. It implements a new education of learning while working. It was established during the summer vacation of this year. Li Shizeng, Wu Zhihui, and others are all members of the school board. The principal is Cui Zhuxi, and the director of academic affairs is Xu Zuoyu. It is currently operating on a trial basis. The funding is subsidized by the Ministry of Education.

Organizational Situation The school is divided into four departments: Library, Publishing, Printing, and Organization. The duration of study for Library and Publishing is six years, and for Printing and Organization is three years. A work-study system is adopted. Classes are held for four hours in the morning, and practical work is done in the afternoon. The Chinese International Library is the workplace for the Library Department, and the World Book Company is the workplace for the Publishing and Printing Departments. The Organization Department is dispatched at any time. Students are divided into two levels: junior high school graduates and senior high school graduates. Students are generally not charged fees. All accommodation, meals, uniforms, books, and supplies are provided by the school. Each month, a living allowance of three to six yuan is given based on the overall grades of each student's academic work, practical work, and conduct.

A Glimpse of the Facilities The school building borrows the Longjiang Building of the World Book Company, and has a library reading room, consumer cooperative, student laundry room, etc. All work in various places is done by the students themselves, so the school employs very few staff. There are only two workers in the whole school.

Student Life The school's student life is very different from other schools. Clothes are washed by the students themselves, and the principal and workers eat the same food. They eat together in the hall, and wash their own bowls and chopsticks. Cleaning the school's buildings is also done by the students. Every place is spotlessly clean, even more so than schools with dozens of workers. Every morning, a military instructor leads them to the riverside to conduct military training and martial arts for one hour, so the students are completely militarized and living a new life.

Daily Schedule Wake up at 5:30 AM, military training at 5:50 AM, morning duties at 6:45 AM, breakfast at 7:15 AM, self-study at 7:30 AM, classes for four hours from 8:30 AM to 11:45 AM, lunch at 12:00 PM, recreation and reading at 12:45 PM, and cooperative sales, practical work from 1:00 PM to 5:00 PM, washing and bathing from 5:00 PM to 5:50 PM, dinner at 6:00 PM, recreation and reading at 7:00 PM, self-study until 8:55 PM, and bedtime at 9:10 PM.

Jinan University Department of Education Prepares to Establish a True Ru Township Teaching Experimental Zone 176

Adopting the Rural Nian Er Society Method

Piloting People's Livelihood-Based Education

True Ru is relatively far from the city, completely a rural area. The population of the entire area is over 10,000, and 90% of them have not received education. In view of this, Shen Pengfei, the president of Jinan University, specially instructed the students of the Department of Education of the university to implement rural education locally. In early spring, a primary school was founded to educate general adults and children. In recent months, it has achieved considerable results. This semester, they are striving to expand it and transform it into a True Ru Township Rural Education Experimental Zone, adopting the Rural Nian Er Society method, piloting people's livelihood-based education and economic activity charts. The organization of the entire area takes the Rural Nian Er Society of each village as the center, and the village chief of each village concurrently serves as the president. Each president further forms a district affairs conference, which is guided by a guidance committee formed by the Department of Education of Jinan University. The Anjia Tu Nongquan Nian Er Society has now been established first, with a view to gradually promoting it, and Ma Jinshen, a graduate of Henan University, has been hired as the facilitator to actively prepare and carry out everything.

Jiangnan University Football Tournament Schedule Set 180

Starts Saturday the 17th

The Jiangnan University Football Tournament is scheduled to begin on Saturday, the 17th of this month. The competition rules and schedule are as follows:

Competition Rules 181

1. A single round-robin system will be used. 2. In each match, the winning team will receive two points, the losing team zero points, and a draw will result in one point for each team. If two teams have the same total score, they will play again. If a draw occurs, the match will be extended by 30 minutes. The date, location, and referee will be appointed by the chairman of the football committee. 3. The rules of the competition will be in accordance with the football rules of the National Games. 4. The referee will be appointed by the home team, but must be agreed upon by the opposing team. If the two sides cannot agree, they may request the committee to appoint one (the home team is responsible for the referee's safety). 5. If there is rain, the venue is not suitable, or in case of emergency, the date may be changed. The date will be notified to the visiting team by the home team with their consent (make-up games must be held before December 31). 6. Each match will start at 2:30 PM. A team that fails to appear 15 minutes before the start of the match will be deemed to have forfeited. However, delays caused by car accidents will not be counted. 7. The list of players must be sent to the chairman of the football committee for review by the committee before November 17. The result of each match must be sent to the chairman of the football committee by the winning team within three days. The list of participating players must be signed by the referee.

Full Schedule 182

November 17: Guanghua at Jinan, Fudan at Chizhi, November 24: Jinan at Chizhi, Fudan at Guanghua, December 1: Fudan at Jinling, Chizhi at Central, December 3: Fudan at Central, Chizhi at Jinling, December 8: Central at Jinling, Fudan at Jinan, Chizhi at Guanghua, December 15: Jinling at Jinan, Central at Guanghua, December 17: Central at Jinan, Jinling at Guanghua

Guangdong Province Holds First Cross-Ridge Race 184

Full Distance of 10.33 Chinese Miles

Time of 17 Minutes and 7.6 Seconds

Thirty-Six People Reached the Finish Line

(Guangzhou Correspondence) The Provincial Capital's First Open Cross-Ridge Race, organized by the Guangdong Provincial People's Sports Experimental Zone, was held on the 4th of this month. Beforehand, the route was measured, and seven checkpoints and six rescue stations were set up along the way. The race route started from the front gate of the Zhongda Linchang in Shipai, crossed the ridge, and ended at the Huangpodong Swimming Pool, with a total distance of 10.33 Chinese miles. Participating groups included the Zhongda Affiliated Middle School, Physical Education School, Panyu Normal School, Nanhai Middle School, Fenggang Elementary School, Central Linchang, Huaxia Middle School, Mingyuan Middle School, Xinhua Vocational School, Land Administration Staff Training Institute, Headquarters Military Band, Fire Brigade Headquarters, Engineering Battalion, Nursing Battalion, Flying Tigers, and other fifteen groups, plus sixteen individuals participating in their own name, totaling seventy-two people. Among them, the middle school sector accounted for forty-three people, and the military sector accounted for sixteen people. The oldest participant was thirty-two years old, and the youngest was sixteen years old. All were male. Because this type of exercise is vigorous, women were not allowed to participate. At around 9:00 AM that morning, the organizers, referees, and inspectors arrived at each station first to perform their duties. At around 10:00 AM, the athletes had gathered at the starting point, and the starter first called the roll. As a result, six people were absent, and sixty-four people actually participated in the competition. The starter then explained the competition rules in detail. At 11:00 AM, the starting gun was fired, and the participants ran together, like ten thousand horses galloping, sand covering the sun. At that time, the race route was pre-arranged with supervisory teams to prevent pedestrians from coming and going. After the runners passed, traffic was restored. At the same time, several ambulances followed to protect them. Those who were found to be unwell and had not reached the finish line were helped into the cars and given medical treatment. The inspectors also paid attention to the runners' running posture at each station. All the athletes had hopes of winning the championship and ran like flying, moving towards the northeast one after another. At that time, those who had gone to Huangpodong to wait and watch had gathered in the tens of thousands. Soon, they saw long-distance runners coming down in a mighty manner, surpassing their peers. The first to reach the finish line was Liu Biao from the Fire Brigade Headquarters, taking 17 minutes and 7.6 seconds. The second place was Xu Guoping (Headquarters Military Band), the third place was Gong Mingxin (Nursing Battalion), the fourth place was Chen Guanzhi (Mingyuan Middle School), the fifth place was Li Yaoxin (Physical Education School), the sixth place was He Zhichao (Engineering Battalion), the seventh place was Xiang Guangqin (Physical Education), the eighth place was Liao Caitai (Engineering Battalion), the ninth place was Liang Weilong (Physical Education), the tenth place was Zhou Zikang (Physical Education), the fourteenth place was Yang Qiwei (individual), the fifteenth place was Zhan Zhiying (Physical Education), the sixteenth place was Wen Zhibiao (Zhongda Linchang), the seventeenth place was Guo Long (individual), the eighteenth place was Tao Rubiao (Nanhai Middle School), the nineteenth place was He Guibiao (Engineering Battalion), the twentieth place was Mo Chenjun (Nursing Battalion), the twenty-first place was Chen Yinglan (Nursing Battalion), the twenty-ninth place was Chen Gang (individual), the twenty-third place was Li Bingyao (Land Administration Institute), the twenty-fourth place was He Yin (Zhongda Linchang), the twenty-fifth place was Li Shihe (individual), the twenty-sixth place was Zhong Yuan (Zhongda Linchang), the twenty-seventh place was Liu Yi (individual), the twenty-eighth place was Chen Mao (Engineering Battalion), the twenty-ninth place was Yi Huanmin (individual), the thirtieth place was Xiao Qingquan (Nursing Battalion), the thirty-first place was Chen Qizhao (Panyu), the thirty-second place was Yi Jianfeng (individual), the thirty-third place was Lin Sicong (Zhongda Affiliated Middle School), the thirty-fourth place was Xu Dechu (Nanhai Affiliated Middle School), the thirty-fifth place was Luo Quande (Engineering Battalion), the thirty-sixth place was Lv Rongzhen (Mingyuan Middle School). All thirty-six people reached the finish line. The awards ceremony was held at noon. After the ceremony, the president of the event presented the prizes. The first to ninth place winners were awarded silver shields or silver cups presented by the political circles, and the tenth to thirty-sixth place winners were awarded commemorative medals.

Business News

Financial Markets: Gold Closes High, Surging Six and a Half Yuan 190

Buying Sentiment Fueled… Short Covering and Turning Bullish Move in Tandem

Gold's overall trend remains consistently prosperous. Regardless of how the overseas markets fare, sentiment remains unperturbed. Consequently, the daily pullback yesterday was minimal, and market conditions were robust. The Central Bank's Customs Gold Unit unexpectedly increased its listing price by 0.24 points, dealing a decisive blow to sellers. Once buying activity ignited, the foreign exchange market tightened accordingly, leading to short covering and bullish reversals. The surge was significant. Initially, overseas silver markets saw the London market contract while the American market rose, leading to a slight appreciation in exchange rates. Although forward silver prices had retreated, London's spot gold declined by 5.5 pence. Off-market pre-market trading opened slightly weaker, retreating to 712 yuan. Eager buyers took advantage of the dip, promptly pushing prices upward. The morning opening reversed and opened higher.

After the opening, the Central Bank's listing prices were announced, with British currency contracting by 0.25 and American currency by 0.50. The gold standard price rose to over 1,000 yuan, and the Customs Gold Unit suddenly surged by 0.24 points, posing a significant threat to sellers. Morale surged, stimulating buying sentiment, and the foreign exchange market also tightened remarkably, rising to 80 yuan. Although major players were still selling at this point, banks had a strong appetite, leading to substantial fluctuations. HSBC's listing prices saw British currency contract by 0.25 and American currency by 0.50, breaking through 80 yuan. Subsequently, the foreign exchange market tightened further, with scarce supply. With major players covering short positions, sellers retreated, and buying sentiment intensified, ultimately pushing prices to over 83 yuan.

Thereafter, with some supply becoming available, Sassoon and others released a limited amount of currency, stabilizing the foreign exchange market and retreating it back within the 80 yuan range. The silver equalization tax remained at 8.15%. British exchange rates were calculated at 1 shilling 5.59379 pence. At this point, the market sought supply equalization, leading to more fluctuations. When the Central Bank released British currency, sentiment was slightly affected, and real users became active, causing a dip. However, the overall trend remained stable, and prices quickly recovered after the initial decline. The Central Bank's reverse hedging of near-term British gold maintained confidence, resulting in a robust situation at noon. Swap trading approached, and views within the industry varied. Before the swap trading began, the bullish sentiment was quite high, with rumors of deals already being made at 1.5 yuan. However, powerful bearish forces were reportedly preparing to liquidate their positions, making it difficult for bulls to be optimistic. When pushing up the market, the sheer volume of inventory may prevent buyers from achieving their anticipated gains.

Currently, with foreign silver prices rising, banks should be able to supply currency readily. However, due to the banks' soft psychology and their fear of a seller rush that could depress silver prices, many are taking a wait-and-see approach, lacking the appetite to sell. For half-day market conditions, it is easier for prices to rise than fall. The half-day market conditions are recorded below:

The morning opening was at 973.8 yuan, an increase of 0.8 yuan compared to the previous day. Although Fuxing Yong sold up to 3 yuan, the Central Bank's Customs Gold increase of 0.24 points stimulated buying sentiment, with Hengyu, Huixiang, Qingyu, Richang, Fuyu, and Dafa Yong competing to buy. The situation gradually rose to 80 yuan. Fuxing Yong offloaded its holdings, dropping to 7.5 yuan. The domestic market had tightened. Meifeng hedged December US dollars at 33.8125 yuan. Richang and Sanfeng competed to buy, pushing prices up to 9.2 yuan. Fuxing Yong, Qingyu, Dafa Yong, Xianghe, and Xiangfeng took advantage of the high prices to offload their holdings, dropping to 7.7 yuan again. Fuxing Yong, Qianchangxiang, and Dingkang negotiated, pushing prices back above 9 yuan. At this point, due to Hengchang Yong, Hengxing, Hongli, and Dalian Bang still selling, prices fell to within 8 yuan. HSBC and others hedged January US dollars at 8125 yuan. Hua Bi purchased December US dollars at 8125 yuan. Senchang Yong, Dafa Yong, Qianchangxiang, Hengyu, and others continued to buy, pushing prices back to 80.5 yuan. The market anticipated HSBC's listing prices, with British currency contracting by 0.25 and American currency declining by 0.50. Fuxing Yong's selling interest remained strong, retreating to 79 yuan. However, the domestic market was extremely tight, and Chinese merchants were eager to hedge but found it difficult. Shortly thereafter, Hua Bi hedged December US dollars again at 75 yuan. With Senchang Yong, Hengyu, Fuchang, Hengxing, Tongchun, and others competing to buy, prices soared to 83.7 yuan. The Central Bank's equalization tax was announced, remaining at 8.25%. After the closing, sellers were slightly eager, causing prices to retreat to within 9 yuan. Demand Exceeds Supply: Foreign Exchange Market Tightens Both Officially and Unofficially 191

According to foreign news reports yesterday, London's major trading saw both near and far contracts contract by 0.375. The US dollar to British pound rate remained unchanged, while the British pound to French franc rate increased by 3 pounds. The US dollar to French franc rate remained unchanged. Mont de Halle's forward silver market retreated by 0.06 points. Reports indicated that the US Treasury Department announced that domestic funds could be freely transferred out of the country. This was perceived as a guarantee of sound currency and an indication that the inflationary sell-off would not recur. The foreign exchange market opened in the morning with near-term selling prices of 1 shilling 4.375 pence for the British pound and 34 yuan for the US dollar. Compared to the previous closing, the British pound had loosened by 0.0625 and the US dollar had tightened by 0.0625. After the opening, with the Central Bank's listing prices showing a contraction of 0.25 for British currency and 0.50 for American currency, and the Customs Gold increase of 0.24 points, Chinese merchants' sentiment remained firm. Banks, in turn, began to hedge, leading to a tightening market. HSBC's listing prices were announced, showing a contraction of 0.25 for British currency and 0.50 for American currency. Banks had an appetite to buy, but Chinese merchants found it difficult to hedge, leading to a further tightening market. However, Sassoon and others took advantage of the high prices to supply currency, leading to a stabilization. Subsequently, the Central Bank also released currency, causing a temporary loosening. Ultimately, due to limited inventory and the Central Bank's reverse hedging of near-term contracts, the market returned to a stable state at noon. Spring and Autumn

Little Western Paradise 205

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Four: A Cup of Water Shows the Difficulty of Seeking, a Poor Laborer Protects the Elderly, Ten Thousand Pieces of Gold Can Be Obtained, a Cunning Official Writes Couplets

Li Shilian smiled and said, "I dare not be conceited about other things, but when it comes to newly established institutions, how to organize them, I am always a bit of an expert." Jia Duocai laughed, "Just go find a way, and once you find a way, we'll have a place to do business, no matter what." "You two talk, I'll see you in the evening." As he spoke, he stood up. Li Shilian saw him come in a hurry, and he must have something to say. Now that he left without saying anything, it seemed that he did not want to say it because there was someone there. So he followed him behind, to the gate of the courtyard, and asked in a low voice, "Duocai, do you have any advice?" Jia Duocai couldn't help laughing and said, "There's nothing to say. I heard that the girl is in the back courtyard, so I came to take a look." Li Shilian laughed and said, "You really haven't forgotten her. If you really mean it, I can help you with it." Jia Duocai laughed and said, "Just acting on the stage, don't take it seriously." With that, he quickly walked away. Li Shilian returned to the room, and Guo Dunpin's first words were, "Does this person have money or not?" Shilian said, "To say he has money in his own hands, I wouldn't say he has much, but he is very active. To move twenty or thirty thousand yuan is no big deal." Guo Dunpin straightened the thumb and little finger of his right hand, compared them on his lips, and asked, "Does he like this?" Then he stretched out both hands, pressed his palms flat, a few inches away from the table, and rubbed them back and forth several times, and said, "Or does he like this?" Li Shilian said, "He doesn't like either of these, he likes women." Guo Dunpin laughed and said, "This thing, I can do it, I'll find two people for him to look at, okay?" Shilian then told him about the refugee girl he had noticed. Guo Dunpin said, "Alas! People from the west road, can they still be saved? If you ask people to come to Little Western Paradise, whether it works out or not, you have to spend a dollar or two on transportation first. I'll just pretend that a friend brought them here, without spending a penny, and let him take a look." (64)

The West Lake Pleasure Boats of the Yuan Dynasty 206

— 19

Mentioning the [West Lake Pleasure Boats], one cannot help but be transported to the Six Bridges and Three Temples. Since the Song Dynasty, West Lake has been praised by people; therefore, it is natural to associate it with pleasure boats. Thus, when ancient people described West Lake, they always depicted it—the pleasure boat—in their writings; there are many such examples, too numerous to record.

Now, everyone knows that there are two types of West Lake pleasure boats: large and small. The smaller ones are simply rowing boats, with sharp ends and covered with cloth awnings. In the middle, they are bordered by copper or rattan railings, and inside there are rattan tables and chairs, simply arranged. The larger ones are shaped like Suzhou speedboats, with windows on the sides, resplendent with gold and jade; they can accommodate many people. This is the style of pleasure boats in recent times. As for what the pleasure boats of ancient times looked like, little is recorded, so much cannot be verified.

I recently read the Zhenju lyrics by Zhang Boyu of the Yuan Dynasty, which contains a poem [Too often lead], which can be used to examine the style of the pleasure boats at that time. It is entitled:

[Man Weng newly made pleasure boats in the lake, I named his boat Floating Home. Weng's surname is Li, named Renzhong, and the use of cloth sails on lake boats began with Li.] The full poem is recorded below:

[Do not compare West Lake to Xizi, a thousand years of Tao Zhu; fearing to live in buildings, also using wind sails and short cattails. Silver bottle asks for wine, and the knife chops the seabass, the boat's back is blurred with brocade. On the embankment, early preaching: [Who is the fisherman of the misty waves?]]

[The use of cloth sails on lake boats began with Li.] From this, we can see that before the Yuan Dynasty, West Lake pleasure boats did not use sails, and we can also prove that [since Li began], there must have been many boats using sails on the lake. The [Floating Home] indicates the size of the boat. The [asking for wine] and [chopping seabass] suggest that the boat could set up banquets, gather guests and drink heartily. From the sentence [the boat's back is blurred with brocade], we can imagine that the boats at that time must have had windows on the sides, and the furnishings inside the boat must have been very rich. The [preaching] shows that the crowd of tourists on the embankment is self-evident.

I therefore think that if the current West Lake pleasure boats could use cloth sails, then the sails would make the lake more secluded and beautiful. However, if the boatmen want to worship their ancestors, then naturally they should promote the old man Li of the Yuan Dynasty.

A Record of Court Hearing 207

— Baling

Going to court to listen to a trial, this is the first time in my life.

It was a late autumn morning, in order to increase my knowledge, I took a car with my colleague Mr. Zhang to the Special Zone Court to be a spectator.

After getting spectator tickets, I sat in the second courtroom, waiting for the trial to begin. Before the trial, I looked around at all kinds of spectators. Some looked worried, as if they had endless things on their minds. Some were talking eloquently, discussing how to deal with the judge's questions. Here, everything seemed silent, revealing the dignity of the court.

The trial began, and everyone bowed to the judge and sat down to listen! I sat for two hours, and I felt that the people being tried were all compatriots from your country with hungry faces, yellow skin and thin bones. And the cases being tried were almost all thefts and other similar situations. This really gave my heart a great stimulus.

I couldn't bear to listen any longer, so I came out with Mr. Zhang. On the way home, I silently thought in my heart: [How should society help these poor compatriots? Passive sanctions ultimately feel unhelpful, and I hope the social authorities will consider this!]

Problems in Child Rearing 208

— Ziwei

Children are the future masters of the country. Their growth, from breastfeeding to leaving the swaddling clothes, receiving education, and reaching various stages of being of service to society and seeking the welfare of the country, completely requires the nurturing and guidance of their fathers, mothers, teachers, good friends.

But how to raise children? Is grammar dependent on means? These are all extremely important small problems.

For example: How do fathers and mothers raise their children? By being overly indulgent? That result is equivalent to killing the child's soul. By strict control? Children have various personalities with innocence, liveliness, and stubbornness. Will they willingly accept instruction? So, how can it be transformed from ugliness, violence, to goodness?

Clear revelation is extremely necessary. If the child goes the wrong way, you have to pull him back and tell him to walk again. What must be walked is the bright avenue. Deception is inappropriate, and indulgence is even more unacceptable. When punishment is due, he should be given a serious lesson. Mama Huhuhu indulges in love and is no different than containing heavy venom that can bury the lives of children.

Recently, I heard that the [Woman's Guidance] film that is being shown in Xinguang has won the praise of the Children's Welfare Association, and it has a very thorough exposure of the problems of children's education. I hope all parents in the world will go and see it.

Yinjuan 209

Walk on the Left 210

— Jin Junren

I don't know about foreign countries, so I dare not say much about the traffic on the roads. In China, most of them walk on the left, not on the right. Qingdao is the only place that walks on the right.

No one can answer why the traffic on the roads in Qingdao must walk on the right. It is said that it was already like this before the takeover. Before the takeover, it was managed by the Japanese, and it was like this during the Japanese management. Before the Japanese, it was managed by the Germans, and it was walking on the right during the German management. So this method has been followed for a long time.

But now the Qingdao Municipal Public Security Bureau has issued a notice that all vehicles, horses, and pedestrians in the city must switch to walking on the left from October 1st of this year. Pedestrians who do not follow this method deserve to die, and vehicles that do not follow this method will be punished.

Chinese people have always had a distinction between high and low for the left and right sides. When people are invited to dinner, they must let the guests sit on the left. In old-fashioned weddings, when the bride and groom bow to each other, the man also stands on the left. Since this is the case, when walking on the road, one naturally has to walk from the left side, and walking from the left side has a meaning of going upward.

The Qingdao Municipal Public Security Bureau has broken decades of habit. Changing from walking on the right to walking on the left is probably also this mentality.

Tidbits 211

— Jin Xiongyu

Bao Gege, the male protagonist of The Story of the Stone, said: A man is made of mud, and a woman is made of water, which means that a man is turbid and a woman is pure; however, if the tide is turbulent and the water splashes, it will stir up the mud at the bottom of the water, and overturn the mud on the shore. Wouldn't it be mixing with the mud?

Imperial Fragrance Drifting Record 212

— Originally written by Princess Deling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

In that small court on the train, the Empress Dowager's throne was specially made: but in the palaces of Shengjing, there were several existing ones prepared, and there was no need to make another one. Although their carvings and decorations are far less exquisite and rich than those in the Beijing palace because of their age and infrequent use, the one that is now placed in the side hall is not so old. Its material is also generally made of red sandalwood, and there is also a red sandalwood screen behind it, inlaid with very precious marble.

On the walls on all sides, there are also paintings of [Great Fortune] patterns, just like on the walls of the train carriage. The authors of these murals are of course those skilled lacquer workers. They like to use very bright colors for the characters or flowers they paint, which inevitably makes them feel too vulgar.

Taking this main hall as an example, or representing all the palaces in Shengjing with this main hall, they are indeed very brilliant: however, if compared with the imperial villa in Rehe, they are inferior in every aspect! I might as well list a few points as an explanation. For example, on the walls, there are only many murals painted here, which are certainly very bright, but how can they be said to be precious and unique? In the imperial villa in Rehe, there are several halls that the Holy Driver often visits, and the walls are covered with various tribute satins: these tribute satins generally also have very beautiful patterns woven on them. Their value is at least ten or twenty times higher than that of paint. Also, in the imperial villa in Rehe, there are many lifelike flying dragons coiled around all the courtyard frames, which are thick enough to be embraced, in several main halls where the Empress Dowager stays each time: they are neither made of wood nor carved from mud, but are originally cast entirely of gold. (174)

Whereabouts

Late Autumn at Ban Yuan 213

— Yan Qiao

Kunshan is not very profound in my imagination. That day, after I and Shoujuan and Xiaoqing watched the chrysanthemums in Qingyang Port, we arrived in Kunshan and found it more ordinary than Tiger Hill in Suzhou. But taking advantage of the fact that the setting sun had not yet fallen below the horizon and the evening colors could still allow us to remember the scenery, we hurriedly went to Ban Yuan for a while, which still makes me feel a little reluctant to this day.

Ban Yuan was called Yuan in the Ming Dynasty, and it was owned by the Ye family, with an area of sixty mu. In the early Qing Dynasty, it was divided into three, and one-third belonged to the Zhong family, so it was called Ban Yuan. But now I estimate that it is not even twenty mu. Because of the good planning of the Sorting Association, it is not considered small. Three open pavilions can be used for tea tasting and social gatherings. There is wireless radio broadcasting, which comes out leisurely from the wall. On the opposite hill, there is a towering Linglong Taihu stone, which is indeed shorter than the Guanyun Peak in Liuyuan Garden in Suzhou, but it also has a long history. It was originally an old object in front of Wang Zhongyu's Kuaizaiting Pavilion in Yangzhou in the Song Dynasty, with an inscription by Su Dongpo. Gu Dehui of the Yuan Dynasty got it from the Xinan Ni Temple in Tongtu Bridge. In the eighth year of the Qing Dynasty, Fang Xian moved it to the garden. This stone is called [Han Cui], and it is inscribed very beautifully, almost as if it were a young girl.

Speaking of young girls, I saw a poem by Gu Tianxi on the wall:

[The wind horse chases the cloud banner, the matter of the gods is even more doubtful, the clear jade earrings reflect the emerald feathers, the fog valley reflects the jade posture; the appearance of Luopu's startled swan, the words that Chen Wang engraved in his heart, diligently laboring in dreams, entrusting the vague thoughts.]

His postscript said that there used to be a statue of the flower god in this garden, with a very beautiful face, but now it is gone, so he is very deeply thoughtful. When I arrived here and read this, I also felt something like that, and wrote a poem to translate for him:

[To see the jagged Han Cui Stone, the setting sun and Autumn England are half new, just have Wu songs coming to the horizon, no need to entrust thoughts to the flower god.]

In the east, there is a crenellated wall, which is short but cleverly reliable for looking into the distance. Who knows that looking into the distance is not as good as looking closely? There is a clear stream outside the wall, and on the opposite bank there is a fisherman sitting peacefully there, lifting a fish trap. Behind him, there are uneven wild trees, and half a field mixed with yellow and green, and in the distance there is a bright sunset, forming a living picture. Unfortunately, the night ruthlessly drove us out of the garden, not allowing us to get any more fun. But it can also be said that it is precisely because of the hurried coming and going that I can still feel a little reluctant to this day.

There are many gardens in Suzhou, and I have been to almost all of them that have a little reputation, but none of them are as petite and exquisite as Ban Yuan, especially with the natural setting and rendering. We feel that this kind of small garden is most suitable for the layout of small cities. At the same time, we also feel that many gardens in Suzhou still need to be reorganized. Like the Ban Yuan Sorting Association, it collects fragments of ancient objects in the city and puts them in the garden, and some of them are used as seats. In this way, every piece of wood and every stone has been given its proper place. I also feel that this can give those who preserve ancient objects and those who engage in construction a reference.
